CREATE DATABASE [HRSystem]
 CONTAINMENT = NONE
 ON  PRIMARY 
( NAME = N'HRSystemDB', FILENAME = N'E:\Databases - Testing\HRSystem.mdf' , SIZE = 8192KB , MAXSIZE = UNLIMITED, FILEGROWTH = 65536KB )
 LOG ON 
( NAME = N'HRSystemDB_log', FILENAME = N'E:\Databases - Testing\HRSystem_log.ldf' , SIZE = 8192KB , MAXSIZE = 2048GB , FILEGROWTH = 65536KB )
 WITH CATALOG_COLLATION = DATABASE_DEFAULT
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[View_Attendance]    Script Date: 21/04/2021 7:02:09 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[View_Attendance]
AS
SELECT DATEPART(month, ar.AttendanceDate) AS Month, DATEPART(yyyy, ar.AttendanceDate) AS Year, emp.firstName + ' ' + emp.Lastname AS [Full Name], post.Pos_Name AS Position, dept.DepartmentName AS Department, lt.LTname AS Classification
FROM   dbo.HR_AttendanceRegister AS ar INNER JOIN
             dbo.HR_tbl_Employee AS emp ON emp.EMP_ID = ar.Emp_Id INNER JOIN
             dbo.HR_tbl_Position AS post ON emp.PosID = post.Pos_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
             dbo.HR_Department AS dept ON dept.DepartmentId = emp.DepartmentID LEFT OUTER JOIN
             dbo.HR_LeaveType AS lt ON lt.LeaveTypeID = ar.AttendLeaveID
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[View_Attendance2]    Script Date: 21/04/2021 7:02:09 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[View_Attendance2] AS SELECT HR_tbl_Employee.firstName + ' ' + HR_tbl_Employee.Lastname AS Name, HR_Department.DepartmentName AS Department, DATEPART(month, HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceDate) AS Month, DATEPART(yyyy, HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceDate) AS Year, 
             HR_tbl_Position.Pos_Name, 'Absent' AS [Classification]
FROM   HR_tbl_TakenLeave INNER JOIN
             HR_AttendanceRegister ON HR_tbl_TakenLeave.AttendanceID = HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceID INNER JOIN
             HR_tbl_Employee ON HR_AttendanceRegister.Emp_Id = HR_tbl_Employee.EMP_ID INNER JOIN
             HR_tbl_Position ON HR_tbl_Employee.PosID = HR_tbl_Position.Pos_ID INNER JOIN
             HR_Department ON HR_tbl_Employee.DepartmentID = HR_Department.DepartmentId
UNION ALL


SELECT HR_tbl_Employee.firstName + ' ' + HR_tbl_Employee.Lastname AS Name, HR_Department.DepartmentName AS Department, DATEPART(month, HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceDate) AS Month, DATEPART(yyyy, HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceDate) AS Year, 
             HR_tbl_Position.Pos_Name, 'Present' AS [Classification]
FROM   HR_tbl_Employee LEFT OUTER JOIN
             HR_Department ON HR_tbl_Employee.DepartmentID = HR_Department.DepartmentId LEFT OUTER JOIN
             HR_AttendanceRegister ON HR_tbl_Employee.EMP_ID = HR_AttendanceRegister.Emp_Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
             HR_tbl_Position ON HR_tbl_Employee.PosID = HR_tbl_Position.Pos_ID

GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[View_Days_Absent]    Script Date: 21/04/2021 7:02:09 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[View_Days_Absent] AS SELECT   HR_tbl_Employee.firstName + ' ' + HR_tbl_Employee.Lastname AS FullName, 
HR_tbl_Position.Pos_Name, 
DATEPART(month, HR_tbl_TakenLeave.leavedate) AS Month, DATEPART(yyyy, HR_tbl_TakenLeave.leavedate) AS Year,
                         HR_Department.DepartmentName,  HR_tbl_TakenLeave.TakenLeaveID
FROM         HR_tbl_Employee INNER JOIN
                         HR_tbl_Position ON HR_tbl_Employee.PosID = HR_tbl_Position.Pos_ID INNER JOIN
                         HR_Department ON HR_tbl_Employee.DepartmentID = HR_Department.DepartmentId INNER JOIN
                         HR_tbl_TakenLeave ON HR_tbl_Employee.EMP_ID = HR_tbl_TakenLeave.EMP_ID
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[View_Days_Worked]    Script Date: 21/04/2021 7:02:09 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[View_Days_Worked] AS SELECT   
HR_tbl_Employee.firstName + ' ' + HR_tbl_Employee.Lastname AS [Full Name], 
HR_tbl_Position.Pos_Name AS [Position], 
DATEPART(month, HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceDate) AS Month, DATEPART(yyyy, HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceDate) AS Year,
HR_Department.DepartmentName,HR_AttendanceRegister.AttendanceID
                          
FROM         HR_tbl_Employee INNER JOIN
                         HR_AttendanceRegister ON HR_tbl_Employee.EMP_ID = HR_AttendanceRegister.Emp_Id INNER JOIN
                         HR_tbl_Position ON HR_tbl_Employee.PosID = HR_tbl_Position.Pos_ID INNER JOIN
                         HR_Department ON HR_tbl_Employee.DepartmentID = HR_Department.DepartmentId
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[spGetDeptAttendance]    Script Date: 21/04/2021 7:02:09 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spGetDeptAttendance]@deptID int
AS
Begin

SELECT TOP (1000) [AttendanceID]
	,ar.[Emp_Id]
	,emp.firstName+' '+emp.Lastname as FullName
	,AttendanceDate
	,[TimeIN]
	,[TimeOUT]
	--,[AttendLeaveID]
	,lt.LTname
	,[note]
	,ar.[DateCreated]
FROM [dbo].[HR_AttendanceRegister] as ar
inner join dbo.HR_tbl_Employee emp on emp.EMP_ID=ar.EMP_Id
left join dbo.HR_Department as dept on dept.DepartmentId=emp.DepartmentID
left join dbo.HR_LeaveType as lt on lt.LeaveTypeID=ar.LeaveTypeID

where dept.DepartmentId=@deptID
order by ar.[AttendanceID] desc
End
GO
